       let avatarUserCx = document.querySelector('#user-popin-cb');
    var timer;
    document.querySelectorAll("label[for='user-popin-cb'], .user-popin").forEach(item => {
      item.addEventListener('mouseenter', event => {
        clearTimeout(timer);
        avatarUserCx.checked = true;
      })
      item.addEventListener('mouseleave', event => {
        timer = setTimeout(function () {
          avatarUserCx.checked = false;

      })

   <script defer="">
    function showCookiesEncourag () {
    var cookiesEncourag = document.getElementById('cookiesEncourag');
    if (cookiesEncourag) {
        cookiesEncourag.style.display = '';

        attag.publisher.set({
            impression: {campaignId: obs_cmp_campaignId  || '[cmp]', creation: '[deny_all]', format: '[desktop]'}
        });
        attag.dispatch();
    }
}

if (typeof Event === 'function') {
    document.documentElement.addEventListener('updateConsentClasses', function(e) {
        showCookiesEncourag();
    });
} else {
    showCookiesEncourag();
}
   </script>
   <script>
    window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {

    var abLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.co-enc__panel__abo,.co-enc__panel__cookies'), i, abLink;
    if (! abLinks || ! abLinks.length) {
        return;
    }
    for (i in abLinks) {
        abLink = abLinks[i];
        console.log(abLink);
        if (typeof abLink.addEventListener !== 'function') {
            continue;
        }
        abLink.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
                var x = new XMLHttpRequest;
    x.open("get", "https://www.nouvelobs.com/r/cookiesEncouragements?u=");
    x.send();
        });
    }

});
   </script>
